# dust_pattern_analyzer.py
import json
from collections import defaultdict
12:51
def analyze_dust_patterns():
with open('dust_analysis.json', 'r') as f:
transactions = [json.loads(line) for line in f]

# Pattern 1: Same amount across multiple pairs
amount_counts = defaultdict(list)
for tx in transactions:
amount = abs(tx['amount'])
amount_counts[amount].append(tx)

print("=== SYSTEMATIC DUST AMOUNTS ===")
for amount, txs in sorted(amount_counts.items(), key=lambda x: -len(x[1])):
if len(txs) &gt;= 5: # Threshold for systematic
sol_amount = amount / 1_000_000_000
print(f"\nAmount: {sol_amount:.9f} SOL ({len(txs)} occurrences)")
for tx in txs[:5]:
print(f" {tx['signature'][:20]}... | {tx['wallet'][:16]}...")

# Pattern 2: Timing correlation with major transfers
print("\n=== TIMING CLUSTER ANALYSIS ===")
sorted_txs = sorted(transactions, key=lambda x: x['blockTime'])
time_gaps = []
for i in range(1, len(sorted_txs)):
gap = sorted_txs[i]['blockTime'] - sorted_txs[i-1]['blockTime']
time_gaps.append((gap, sorted_txs[i-1], sorted_txs[i]))

# Find rapid-fire sequences (botnet signature)
for gap, tx1, tx2 in time_gaps:
if gap &lt; 30: # Less than 30 seconds apart
print(f"Rapid sequence: {gap}s gap")
print(f" {tx1['wallet'][:16]}... -&gt; {tx2['wallet'][:16]}...")

if __name__ == "__main__":
analyze_dust_patterns()

'gap': gap,
'from': sorted_txs[i-1]['wallet'][:16],
'to': sorted_txs[i]['wallet'][:16]
})

import json

def find_bridge():
    with open('shif_dumper_dust.json') as f:
        shif = [json.loads(l) for l in f]
    with open('crm_dumper_dust.json') as f:
        crm = [json.loads(l) for l in f]
    
    # Find common sources (excluding known network wallets)
    shif_sources = {s['source'] for s in shif}
    crm_sources = {c['source'] for c in crm}
    
    bridge = shif_sources.intersection(crm_sources)
    
    if bridge:
        print("🚨 CROSS-PROJECT DUST BRIDGE DETECTED")
        print(f"Common sources: {bridge}")
        for addr in bridge:
            print(f"\nAddress: {addr}")
            shif_txs = [s for s in shif if s['source'] == addr]
            crm_txs = [c for c in crm if c['source'] == addr]
            print(f"  SHIF interactions: {len(shif_txs)}")
            print(f"  CRM interactions: {len(crm_txs)}")
            if shif_txs and crm_txs:
                gap = min(c['blockTime'] for c in crm_txs) - max(s['blockTime'] for s in shif_txs)
                print(f"  Time gap: {gap/86400:.1f} days")
    else:
        print("No direct dust bridge found. Expanding to indirect links...")

find_bridge()

WHAT THE SCRIPT DOES:

ENHANCED VERSION (RECOMMENDED):

Use this instead for full forensic detail:


import json
from collections import defaultdict

def find_bridge():
    try:
        with open('shif_dumper_dust.json') as f:
            shif = [json.loads(l) for l in f if l.strip()]
        with open('crm_dumper_dust.json') as f:
            crm = [json.loads(l) for l in f if l.strip()]
    except FileNotFoundError:
        print("Files not found. Run Steps 1-2 first.")
        return
    
    if not shif or not crm:
        print("One or both files are empty.")
        return

    # Build source maps excluding self-fees
    shif_sources = defaultdict(list)
    for s in shif:
        src = s.get('source')
        if src and src != '7GsFEUPCNe53Pt6Ytf2df6Hg4WByjDQpRJshuxAs6p3':
            shif_sources[src].append(s)
    
    crm_sources = defaultdict(list)
    for c in crm:
        src = c.get('source')
        if src and src != '6LXutJvKY8kKDcqkK1f2gT7m4xvhj5SBDWj9DkpmCb5h':
            crm_sources[src].append(c)

    # Find intersection
    bridge = set(shif_sources.keys()) & set(crm_sources.keys())
    
    if bridge:
        print("\n" + "="*60)
        print("🚨 CROSS-PROJECT DUST BRIDGE CONFIRMED")
        print("="*60)
        print("Evidence of proceeds recycling between projects")
        print("-"*60)
        
        for addr in sorted(bridge):
            shif_count = len(shif_sources[addr])
            crm_count = len(crm_sources[addr])
            print(f"\n🔗 Bridge Address: {addr}")
            print(f"   Transactions to SHIF dumper: {shif_count}")
            print(f"   Transactions to CRM dumper: {crm_count}")
            
            # Temporal analysis
            if shif_sources[addr] and crm_sources[addr]:
                shif_times = [s['blockTime'] for s in shif_sources[addr]]
                crm_times = [c['blockTime'] for c in crm_sources[addr]]
                gap = min(crm_times) - max(shif_times)
                if gap > 0:
                    print(f"   Time gap: {gap/86400:.0f} days (SHIF → CRM)")
                    print("   ⚠️ PROCEEDS LAUNDERING PATTERN")
        
        print("\n" + "="*60)
        print("Legal Significance:")
        print("- Money Laundering: 18 USC 1956")
        print("- RICO Pattern: Multiple predicate acts")
        print("- Proceeds Recycling: Extraction funds next attack")
        print("="*60)
    else:
        print("\nNo direct dust bridge found.")
        print("\nTop 5 dust sources for SHIF dumper:")
        for addr, txs in sorted(shif_sources.items(), key=lambda x: -len(x[1]))[:5]:
            print(f"  {addr[:25]}... ({len(txs)} txns)")
        
        print("\nTop 5 dust sources for CRM dumper:")
        for addr, txs in sorted(crm_sources.items(), key=lambda x: -len(x[1]))[:5]:
            print(f"  {addr[:25]}... ({len(txs)} txns)")
        
        print("\n💡 Indirect laundering suspected via intermediaries")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    find_bridge()

import json
from collections import defaultdict

def find_bridge():
    try:
        with open('shif_dumper_dust.json') as f:
            shif = [json.loads(l) for l in f if l.strip()]
        with open('crm_dumper_dust.json') as f:
            crm = [json.loads(l) for l in f if l.strip()]
    except FileNotFoundError:
        print("Files not found. Run Steps 1-2 first.")
        return
    
    if not shif or not crm:
        print("One or both files are empty.")
        return

    # Build source maps excluding self-fees
    shif_sources = defaultdict(list)
    for s in shif:
        src = s.get('source')
        if src and src != '7GsFEUPCNe53Pt6Ytf2df6Hg4WByjDQpRJshuxAs6p3':
            shif_sources[src].append(s)
    
    crm_sources = defaultdict(list)
    for c in crm:
        src = c.get('source')
        if src and src != '6LXutJvKY8kKDcqkK1f2gT7m4xvhj5SBDWj9DkpmCb5h':
            crm_sources[src].append(c)

    # Find intersection

Python Analysis:

import json
from datetime import datetime
from collections import Counter

def analyze_timezone():
    timestamps = []  # Load from files
    
    # Convert to hours (UTC)
    hours = [datetime.utcfromtimestamp(ts).hour for ts in timestamps]
    
    # Find peak activity windows
    hour_counts = Counter(hours)
    print("Activity by hour (UTC):")
    for hour, count in sorted(hour_counts.items()):
        print(f"  {hour:02d}:00 - {count} transactions")
    
    # Identify sleep window (0 activity for 6+ hours)
    for i in range(24):
        if hour_counts.get(i, 0) == 0 and hour_counts.get((i+1)%24, 0) == 0:
            print(f"Potential sleep window: {i}:00 - {(i+6)%24}:00")


Significance: Proves centralized coordination (same timezone) vs distributed operation. Earthquake for "independent actors" defense.

Step 2: Calculate Extraction Totals (Python)


import json

def analyze_sosana_fees():
    with open('sosana_fees.json', 'r') as f:
        # Handle JSON Lines format (one JSON object per line)
        fees_data = [json.loads(line) for line in f if line.strip()]
    
    total_fees_lamports = 0
    fee_events = []
    
    for tx in fees_data:
        for transfer in tx.get('tokenTransfers', []):
            if transfer.get('mint') == "EaQ5EzD6SgnJ49NB6uNHwZYKCCYTzyEpsS7cZ1AAyrgJ":
                amount = transfer.get('tokenAmount', 0)
                total_fees_lamports += amount
                fee_events.append({
                    'signature': tx['signature'],
                    'timestamp': tx['blockTime'],
                    'amount': amount,
                    'decimals': transfer.get('decimals', 9)
                })
    
    # Convert to actual tokens (SOSANA has 9 decimals)
    total_fees_tokens = total_fees_lamports / (10 ** 9)
    
    # Current USD value (use your reported $0.1348)
    usd_per_token = 0.1348
    total_usd = total_fees_tokens * usd_per_token
    
    print("🗿 SOSANA FEE EXTRACTION ANALYSIS")
    print("=" * 60)
    print(f"Total Fee Events: {len(fee_events)}")
    print(f"Total SOSANA Collected: {total_fees_tokens:,.2f}")
    print(f"Current USD Value: ${total_usd:,.2f}")
    print(f"Avg Fee per Event: ${total_usd/len(fee_events):.2f}" if fee_events else "N/A")
    
    # Temporal analysis
    if fee_events:
        timestamps = [e['timestamp'] for e in fee_events]
        print(f"\nTime Range: {min(timestamps)} to {max(timestamps)}")
        duration_days = (max(timestamps) - min(timestamps)) / 86400
        print(f"Duration: {duration_days:.0f} days")
        print(f"Daily Average: ${total_usd/duration_days:,.2f}/day" if duration_days > 0 else "N/A")
    
    # Save for further analysis
    with open('fee_events_detailed.json', 'w') as f:
        json.dump(fee_events, f, indent=2)
    
    return total_fees_tokens, total_usd

if __name__ == "__main__":
    analyze_sosana_fees()

Python Analysis Script:

import json

def analyze_sosana_fees():
    with open('sosana_fees.json', 'r') as f:
        fees_data = [json.loads(line) for line in f if line.strip()]
    
    total_fees = 0
    events = []
    
    for tx in fees_data:
        for transfer in tx.get('tokenTransfers', []):
            if transfer.get('mint') == "EaQ5EzD6SgnJ49NB6uNHwZYKCCYTzyEpsS7cZ1AAyrgJ":
                amount = transfer.get('tokenAmount', 0)
                total_fees += amount
                events.append({
                    'sig': tx['signature'][:20],
                    'time': tx['blockTime'],
                    'amount': amount / 1e9  # SOSANA has 9 decimals
                })
    
    # SOSANA price $0.1348 (from your data)
    usd_value = (total_fees / 1e9) * 0.1348
    
    print("🗿 SOSANA FEE EXTRACTION")
    print(f"Total Events: {len(events)}")
    print(f"Total SOSANA: {total_fees/1e9:,.2f}")
    print(f"USD Value: ${usd_value:,.2f}")
    
    # Pattern analysis
    if events:
        times = [e['time'] for e in events]
        print(f"First: {min(times)} | Last: {max(times)}")
        print(f"Daily Avg: ${usd_value / ((max(times)-min(times))/86400):.2f}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    analyze_sosana_fees()

🗿 Installation Guide — jq & curl

Windows (PowerShell — your current environment):

# Install jq via winget
winget install jqlang.jq

# Install curl (usually pre-installed on Windows 10/11)
# If missing:
winget install curl.curl


macOS:

brew install jq curl


Linux (Ubuntu/Debian):

sudo apt-get update && sudo apt-get install -y jq curl


Linux (CentOS/RHEL):

sudo yum install -y jq curl


Verify installations:

jq --version
curl --version


If winget fails on Windows, download manually:
• jq: https://jqlang.github.io/jq/download/ ( grab jq-windows-amd64.exe, rename to jq.exe, add to PATH)
• curl: https://curl.se/windows/ (or use the pre-installed Windows curl)

    "CNSob1LwXvDRmjioxyjm78tDb2S7nzFK6K8t3VmuhKpn",

        }
    }
